85        /**
86         *  Return the publisher object that other in-process services can register with to listen
87         *  for specific property change events.
88         */
89        public synchronized TradingPropertyPublisher getTradingPropertyPublisher()
90        {
91            if (tradingPropertyPublisher == null)
92            {
93                        tradingPropertyPublisher = new TradingPropertyPublisherLocalImpl();
94                        // Connect cache manager to event channel:
95                        //
96            ChannelKey key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.ALL_TRADING_PROPERTY, new Integer(0));
97            try {
98                 EventHomes.getTradingPropertyConsumerHome().addConsumer(tradingPropertyPublisher, key);
99             }
100             catch (Exception e) {
101                 Log.exception(this, "Unable to connect consumer to event channel", e);
102             }
103             }
104 
105             return tradingPropertyPublisher;
106        }
107 
108        /**

110         *  for specific property change events.
111         */

113        {
114           return (TradingPropertyPublisherExt)getTradingPropertyPublisher();
115        }

137        /**
138         *  Admin request to get trading property
139         */
140        public String adminGetTradingProperty(String propertyName, String sessionName, String classKeyString)
141        {
142                java.io.StringWriter writer = new java.io.StringWriter();
143                try
144                {
145                        org.omg.CORBA.IntHolder intHolder = new org.omg.CORBA.IntHolder();
146                        int classKey = 0;
147                        boolean allClassString = false;
148 
149                        if (classKeyString != null && classKeyString.trim().length() > 0 && !classKeyString.equalsIgnoreCase("default"))
150                        {
151                                classKey = Integer.parseInt(classKeyString);
152                        }
153 
154                        writer.write("Results from \"get\":\n");
155 
156                        if (propertyName.equalsIgnoreCase("ExchangePrescribedWidth"))
157                        {
158                                EPWStruct[] result = getExchangePrescribedWidth(sessionName, classKey, intHolder);
159                                ReflectiveStructBuilder.printStruct(result, "EPWStructs", writer);
160                        }
161                        else if (propertyName.equalsIgnoreCase("MinSizeForBlockTrade"))
162                        {
163                                writer.write("Property value = " + getMinSizeForBlockTrade(sessionName, classKey, intHolder) + "\n");
164                        }
165                        else if (propertyName.equalsIgnoreCase("MinQuoteCreditDefaultSize"))
166                        {
167                                writer.write("Property value = " + getMinQuoteCreditDefaultSize(sessionName, intHolder) + "\n");
168                        }
169                        else if (propertyName.equalsIgnoreCase("RFQResponseRatio"))
170                        {
171                                writer.write("Property value = " + getRFQResponseRatio(sessionName, intHolder));
172                        }
173                        else if (propertyName.equalsIgnoreCase("RFQTimeout"))
174                        {
175                                writer.write("Property value = " + getRFQTimeout(sessionName, classKey, intHolder) + "\n");
176                        }
177                        else if (propertyName.equalsIgnoreCase("ContinuousQuotePeriodForCredit"))
178                        {
179                                writer.write("Property value = " + getContinuousQuotePeriodForCredit(sessionName, intHolder) + "\n");
180                        }
181                        else if (propertyName.equalsIgnoreCase("DPMParticipationPercentage"))
182                        {
183                                writer.write("Property value = " + getDPMParticipationPercentage(sessionName, classKey, intHolder) + "\n");
184                        }
185                        else if (propertyName.equalsIgnoreCase("PrescribedWidthRatio"))
186                        {
187                                writer.write("Property value = " + getPrescribedWidthRatio(sessionName, intHolder) + "\n");
188                        }

193                        else if (propertyName.equalsIgnoreCase("AllocationStrategies"))
194                        {
195                            AllocationStrategyStructV2[] strategies = getAllocationStrategies(sessionName, classKey, intHolder);
196 
197                            // format is type1=defaultcode;priority1;priority2,type1=defaultcode;priority1;priority2
198                            // example: 0=1;4;9;7,1=1;8;7,2=1;3;5
199                            StringBuffer codes = new StringBuffer();
200                            for(int i = 0; i < strategies.length; i++)
201                            {
202                                if(i != 0)
203                                {
204                                    codes.append(",");
205                                }
206                                codes.append("" + strategies[i].allocationTradeType);
207                                codes.append("=" + strategies[i].defaultStrategyCode);
208                                for (int j = 0; j < strategies[i].prioritizedStrategyCodes.length; j++) {
209                                    codes.append(";" + strategies[i].prioritizedStrategyCodes[j]);
210                                }
211                            }
212                            writer.write("Property value = " + codes.toString() + "\n");
213                        }

705                    ||  (TradingPropertyFactoryHome.find().getPropertyTypeAllClassesName(propertyName) != 0)
706                    )
707            {
708                PropertyServiceHome priopertyServiceHome = getPropertyServiceHome();
709 
710                if( PropertyTradingPropertyServiceHome.class.isInstance( propertyServiceHome ) )
711                {

713                    String results = propertyTradingPriopertyServiceHome.adminGetTradingProperty( propertyName, sessionName, ""+classKey );
714                    writer.write( results );
715                    return writer.toString();
716                }
717                else
718                {
719                    return "PropertyServiceHome NOT instance of PropertyTradingPropertySerivceHome ==>> Unsupported property type: " + propertyName;
720                }
721            }
722            else
723            {
724                return "Unsupported property type: " + propertyName;
725            }
726 
727            if (allClassString == false)
728            {
729               writer.write("ClassKey       = " + classKey + "\n" + "Sequence       = " + intHolder.value + "\n");
730             }
731             allClassString = false;
732             return writer.toString();
733            }
734            catch (DataValidationException ex)
735            {
736                return "Invalid data: " + ex.details.message;
737            }
738            catch (NotFoundException ex)
739            {
740                return "Property not found: " + ex.details.message;
741            }
742            catch (java.io.IOException ex)
743            {
744                return "Unexpected IO error writing result to string: " + ex;
745            }
746            catch (Throwable ex)
747            {
748                writer.write("TradingPropertyService admin callback error:\n");
749                java.io.PrintWriter printWriter = new java.io.PrintWriter(writer, true/*autoflush*/);
750                ex.printStackTrace(printWriter);
751                return writer.toString();
752            }
753        }
754 
755        /**
756         *  Admin request to set trading property
757         *  Added remove method invoked from setTradingProperty script
758         */
759        public String adminSetTradingProperty(String propertyName, String sessionName, String classKeyString, String value, String seqString)
760        {
761                try
762                {
763 
764                        org.omg.CORBA.IntHolder intHolder = new org.omg.CORBA.IntHolder();
765                        int classKey = 0;
766                        int seq = Integer.parseInt(seqString);
767                        String setClassString;
768                        boolean removeClassString = false;
769 
770 
771                        if (classKeyString != null && classKeyString.trim().length() > 0 && !classKeyString.equalsIgnoreCase("default"))
772                        {
773                                classKey = Integer.parseInt(classKeyString);
774                        }
775 
776                        if (propertyName.equalsIgnoreCase("RemoveTradingProperty"))
777                        {
778                            // check if it should use property service, as we always should.  It knows how to do
779                            // add, update and delete for a given trading property that was used to be maintained
780                            // by this class.
781 
782                            // please note that all trading properties type and names should be defined
783                            // for PropertyService in TradingPropertyTypeImpl.
784                            // new trading property should also be added to TradingPropertyFactoryImpl
785 
786                            if( TradingPropertyFactoryHome.find().getPropertyType( value ) != 0 )
787                            {
788                                PropertyServiceHome priopertyServiceHome = getPropertyServiceHome();
789 
790                                if( PropertyTradingPropertyServiceHome.class.isInstance( propertyServiceHome ) )
791                                {
792                                    PropertyTradingPropertyServiceHome propertyTradingPropertyServiceHome = (PropertyTradingPropertyServiceHome) propertyServiceHome;
793                                    return propertyTradingPropertyServiceHome.adminSetTradingProperty( propertyName, sessionName,
794                                            "" + classKey, value, "" + seq );
795                                }
796                                else
797                                {
798                                    return "PropertyServiceHome NOT instance of PropertyTradingPropertySerivceHome ==>> Unsupported property type: "
799                                    + propertyName;
800                                }
801                            }
802 
803                            // this should never been executed as we should start to use property service to do any
804                            // updates and removal.  Alarm is logged inside of the removeTradingProperty method.
805 
806                            int propertyType = Integer.parseInt( value );
807                            removeTradingProperty( sessionName, classKey, propertyType );
808                            removeClassString = true;
809                        }
810                        else if (propertyName.equalsIgnoreCase("PrescribedWidthRatio"))
811                        {
812                                double doubleValue = Double.parseDouble(value);
813                                System.out.println("Set prescribed width ratio to "+ doubleValue);
814                                if (classKey != 0) {
815                                    setPrescribedWidthRatio(sessionName, classKey, Double.parseDouble(value), seq);
816                                }
817                                else {
818                                    setPrescribedWidthRatio(sessionName, Double.parseDouble(value), seq);
819                                }
820                        }
821                        else if (propertyName.equalsIgnoreCase("DPMParticipationPercentage"))
822                        {
823                                setDPMParticipationPercentage(sessionName, classKey, Double.parseDouble(value), seq);
824                        }
825                        else if (propertyName.equalsIgnoreCase("FastMarketSpreadMultiplier"))
826                        {
827                                setFastMarketSpreadMultiplier(sessionName, classKey, Double.parseDouble(value), seq);
828                        }
829 
830                        else if (propertyName.equalsIgnoreCase("AllocationStrategies"))
831                        {
832                            StringTokenizer structTokens = new StringTokenizer(value, ",");
833                            ArrayList structList = new ArrayList();
834                            while (structTokens.hasMoreTokens())
835                            {
836                                String structString = structTokens.nextToken();
837                                StringTokenizer typeTokens = new StringTokenizer(structString, "=");
838                                AllocationStrategyStructV2 struct = new AllocationStrategyStructV2();
839 
840                                struct.allocationTradeType = Short.parseShort(typeTokens.nextToken());
841                                String codesString = typeTokens.nextToken();
842                                StringTokenizer codeTokens = new StringTokenizer(codesString, ";");
843                                String curValue = codeTokens.nextToken();
844                                struct.defaultStrategyCode = Short.parseShort(curValue);
845                                int size = codeTokens.countTokens();
846                                struct.prioritizedStrategyCodes = new short[size];
847                                for (int i = 0; i < size; i++) {
848                                    curValue = codeTokens.nextToken();
849                                    struct.prioritizedStrategyCodes[i] = Short.parseShort(curValue);
850                                }
851                                structList.add(struct);
852                            }
853 
854                            AllocationStrategyStructV2[] result = new AllocationStrategyStructV2[structList.size()];
855                            structList.toArray(result);
856 
857                            setAllocationStrategies(sessionName, classKey, result, seq);
858                        }

866                                try
867                                {
868                                        StringTokenizer structTokens = new StringTokenizer(value, ";");
869                                        ArrayList epwList = new ArrayList(5);
870                                        while (structTokens.hasMoreTokens())
871                                        {
872                                                String structString = structTokens.nextToken();
873                                                StringTokenizer valueTokens = new StringTokenizer(structString, ",");
874                                                EPWStruct epw = new EPWStruct();
875                                                epw.minimumBidRange = Double.parseDouble(valueTokens.nextToken());
876                                                epw.maximumBidRange = Double.parseDouble(valueTokens.nextToken());
877                                                epw.maximumAllowableSpread = Double.parseDouble(valueTokens.nextToken());
878                                                epwList.add(epw);
879                                        }
880                                        EPWStruct[] structs = new EPWStruct[epwList.size()];
881                                        epwList.toArray(structs);
882                                        setExchangePrescribedWidth(sessionName, classKey, structs, seq);
883                                }
884                                catch (NoSuchElementException ex)
885                                {
886                                        return "Invalid epw struct format string: " + expectedFormat;
887                                }
888                                catch (NumberFormatException ex)
889                                {
890                                        return "Invalid epw struct format string: " + expectedFormat;
891                                }
892                        }
893                        else if (propertyName.equalsIgnoreCase("OpeningPeriodTimeRange"))
894                        {
895                                TimeRangeStruct struct = new TimeRangeStruct();
896                                try

899                                        struct.lowerLimit = Integer.parseInt(tokens.nextToken());
900                                        struct.upperLimit = Integer.parseInt(tokens.nextToken());
901                                }
902                                catch (NoSuchElementException ex)
903                                {
904                                        return "Invalid time range format: expected lowerLimit,upperLimit (integers)";
905                                }
906                                catch (NumberFormatException ex)
907                                {
908                                        return "Invalid time range format: expected lowerLimit,upperLimit (integers)";
909                                }
910                                if (classKey != 0) {
911                                    setOpeningPeriodTimeRange(sessionName, classKey, struct, seq);
912                                }

1465 
1466        /**
1467         *  Register callbacks with the admin callback service.
1468         */
1469        protected void registerCallbacks()
1470                throws com.cboe.infrastructureServices.foundationFramework.exceptionHandling.CBOELoggableException
1471        {
1472            final String properties = getAllPropertyString();
1473            BOHome myHome = getBOHome();
1474 
1475            myHome.registerCommand( this, "setTradingProperty", "adminSetTradingProperty", "set a trading property",
1476                    new String[] { "java.lang.String", "java.lang.String", "java.lang.String", "java.lang.String", "java.lang.String" },
1477                    new String[] { "property: one of " + properties, "sessionName", "classKey (# or \"default\")", "propertyValue", "sequence#" });
1478 
1479            myHome.registerCommand( this, "getTradingProperty", "adminGetTradingProperty", "get a trading property",

1661    private void validateAllocationTradeType(short tradeType) throws DataValidationException
1662    {
1663        // verify tvalid.
1664            Field [] fields = AllocationTradeTypes.class.getFields();
1665            boolean valid = false;
1666            for (int j = 0; j< fields.length; j++)
1667            {
1668                try
1669                {
1670                    if ( tradeType== fields[j].getShort(AllocationTradeTypes.class))
1671                    {
1672                        valid = true;
1673                        break;
1674                    }
1675                }
1676                catch (IllegalAccessException e)
1677                {
1678                    Log.exception(this, "Could not access the field of AllocationTradeTypes " + fields[j].toString(), e);
1679                }
1680            }
1681            if (! valid)
1682            {
1683                throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Invalid allocation trade type" + tradeType, 0);
1684            }
1685    }
1686 
1687    private void validateDefaultStrategyCode(short defaultStrategyCode) throws DataValidationException
1688    {
1689         // verify that default code is valid.
1690        boolean isDefault = isDefaultStrategyCode(defaultStrategyCode);
1691        if (!isDefault)
1692        {
1693            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Invalid default strategy code", 0);
1694        }
1695    }
1696 
1697    private boolean isDefaultStrategyCode(short defaultStrategyCode)
1698    {
1699        boolean isDefault = false;
1700        switch (defaultStrategyCode)
1701        {
1702        case AllocationStrategyCodes.PRICE_TIME:
1703        case AllocationStrategyCodes.PRO_RATA:
1704        case AllocationStrategyCodes.LOCK_MINIMUM_TRADE:
1705             {
1706                isDefault = true;
1707                break;
1708             }
1709        default:
1710        }
1711        return isDefault;
1712    }
1713 
1714    private void validatePrioritizedStrategyCodes(short[] prioritizedStrategyCodes) throws DataValidationException
1715    {
1716       // verify that all of the prioritized codes are valid.  It is OK if none are specified.
1717        for (int i = 0; i < prioritizedStrategyCodes.length; i++)
1718        {
1719            Field [] fields = AllocationStrategyCodes.class.getFields();
1720            boolean valid = false;
1721            for (int j = 0; j< fields.length; j++)
1722            {
1723                try
1724                {
1725                    if ( prioritizedStrategyCodes[i] == fields[j].getShort(AllocationStrategyCodes.class))
1726                    {
1727                        if (!isDefaultStrategyCode(prioritizedStrategyCodes[i]))
1728                        {
1729                            valid = true;
1730                        }
1731                        break;
1732                    }
1733                }
1734                catch (IllegalAccessException e)
1735                {
1736                    Log.exception(this, "Could not access the field of AllocationStrategyCodes " + fields[j].toString(), e);
1737                }
1738            }
1739            if (! valid)
1740            {
1741                throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Invalid priority strategy code: " + prioritizedStrategyCodes[i], 0);
1742            }
1743        }
1744    }
1745    /**
1746     * Validates the allocation strategy.
1747     */
1748    protected void validateAllocationStrategy(AllocationStrategyStruct strategy) throws DataValidationException
1749    {
1750        validateDefaultStrategyCode(strategy.defaultStrategyCode);
1751        validatePrioritizedStrategyCodes(strategy.prioritizedStrategyCodes);
1752    }
1753        /**
1754         *  Throw a DatavalidationException if the given exchange key is invalid.
1755         */
1756        protected void validateSessionName(String sessionName)
1757                throws DataValidationException, SystemException
1758        {
1759                try
1760                {
1761                        getTradingSessionHome().find(sessionName);
1762                }
1763                catch (NotFoundException ex)
1764                {
1765                        throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Session not found: " + sessionName, DataValidationCodes.INVALID_SESSION);
1766                }
1767        }
1768 
1769        /**
1770         *  Throw a DatavalidationException if the given class key is invalid.
1771         */
1772        protected void validateClassKey(int classKey)
1773                throws CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, SystemException
1774        {
1775                if (classKey != ProductClass.DEFAULT_CLASS_KEY)
1776                {
1777                        try
1778                        {
1779                // Using the PQS caused a call loop - TPS called PQS to get class, PQS called TPS to get
1780                // EPW.  Call to PQS was changed to a call to ProductClassHome to break this loop.
1781                                getProductClassHome().findByKey(classKey);
1782                        }
1783                        catch (NotFoundException ex)
1784                        {
1785                                throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Invalid class key " + classKey, DataValidationCodes.INVALID_PRODUCT);
1786                        }
1787                }
1788        }
1789 
1790        /**
1791         *  Find & update sequence id for the given property (assumed to be DEFAULT_CLASS_KEY for classKey).
1792         *  The new sequence number passed in is expected to be one more than the number currently stored with the property,
1793         *  or 0 if this is expected to be a new property instance.
1794         *  This method also performs an exchangeKey validation check.
1795         *  This method will create a persistent property object if one exists already (if seq == 0).
1796         *
1797         *  Return the <code>TradingProperty</code> that was found/created.
1798         */
1799        protected TradingProperty propertyUpdate(String sessionName, int propertyType, int seq)
1800                throws CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, SystemException, DataValidationException, TransactionFailedException
1801        {
1802                return propertyUpdate(sessionName, ProductClass.DEFAULT_CLASS_KEY, propertyType, seq);
1803        }
1804 
1805    /**
1806     *  Refactored code to work with allocation methods
1807     */
1808        protected AllocationStrategyStruct getAllocationStrategyCodes(TradingProperty[] properties)
1809                  throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotFoundException
1810        {
1811            AllocationStrategyStruct result = new AllocationStrategyStruct();
1812            if (properties.length == 1) {
1813                result.defaultStrategyCode = ( (AllocationStrategy) properties[0]).
1814                    getCode();
1815                result.prioritizedStrategyCodes = new short[0];
1816            }
1817            else {
1818                result.prioritizedStrategyCodes = new short[properties.length - 1];
1819                AllocationStrategy strategyProperty;
1820                for (int i = 0; i < properties.length; i++) {
1821                    strategyProperty = (AllocationStrategy) properties[i];
1822                    if (strategyProperty.getIndex() == -1) {
1823                        result.defaultStrategyCode = strategyProperty.getCode();
1824                    }
1825                    else {
1826                        result.prioritizedStrategyCodes[strategyProperty.getIndex()] =
1827                            strategyProperty.getCode();
1828                    }
1829                }
1830            }
1831            return result;
1832        }

1837    }

1844    protected void logPropertyRemoved(TradingProperty property)
1845    {
1846        logPropertyRemoved(property.toString());
1847    }
1848 
1849    protected void logPropertyRemoved(String removedPropertyString)
1850    {
1851        Log.information(this, REMOVE_HEADER + removedPropertyString);
1852    }
1853        /**
1854         *  Find & update sequence id for the given property.
1855         *  The new sequence number passed in is expected to be the number currently stored with the property,
1856         *  or 0 if this is expected to be a new property instance.
1857         *  The new sequence number is passed back through the <code>setInt(int)</code> method of the <code>seq</code> parameter.
1858         *  This method also performs exchangeKey & classKey validation checks.
1859         *  This method will create a persistent property object if one exists already (if seq == 0).
1860         *
1861         *  Return the <code>TradingProperty</code> that was found/created.
1862         */
1863        protected synchronized TradingProperty propertyUpdate(String sessionName, int classKey, int propertyType, int seq)
1864                throws CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, TransactionFailedException, SystemException, DataValidationException
1865        {
1866                validateSessionName(sessionName);
1867                validateClassKey(classKey);
1868                TradingProperty property = null;
1869                int newSeq = 0;
1870                try
1871                {
1872                        property = getTradingPropertyHome().findProperty(sessionName, classKey, propertyType);
1873                        newSeq = property.getSequenceId();
1874                }
1875                catch (NotFoundException ex)
1876                {
1877            // This is ok, but the sequence id passed to this method should be 0.
1878            seq = 0;
1879                }
1880                catch (SystemException ex)
1881                {
1882                        Log.alarm(this, "SystemException in update sequence: " + ex.details.message);
1883                        throw ex;
1884                }
1885 
1886                if (newSeq != seq)
1887                {
1888                        Log.information(this, "Sequence ID out-of-order: expected " + newSeq + ", got " + seq);
1889                        throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Sequence Id out-of-order. Expected " + newSeq + ", got " + seq,
1890                                                                       DataValidationCodes.INVALID_UPDATE_ATTEMPT);
1891                }
1892                boolean committed = false;
1893        boolean isUpdating = true;
1894                Transaction.startTransaction();
1895                try
1896                {
1897                        if (property == null) // create the persistent property.
1898                        {
1899                isUpdating = false;
1900                property = getTradingPropertyHome().createProperty(sessionName, propertyType);
1901                                property.getPersistentProperty().setClassKey(classKey);
1902                        }
1903            if(isUpdating)
1904            {
1905                Log.information(this,  UPDATE_HEADER + property.getPropertyTypeDescription() + ". Existing values: " + property.toString());
1906            }
1907            else    // is creating
1908            {
1909                Log.information(this,  CREATE_HEADER + property.getPropertyTypeDescription() + " for sessionName: " + sessionName + " classKey: " + classKey);
1910            }
1911            property.setSequenceId(++newSeq);
1912                        committed = Transaction.commit();
1913                 }
1914                catch (SystemException ex)
1915                {
1916                        if (property == null)
1917                        {
1918                                throw ExceptionBuilder.transactionFailedException("Persistence exception: " + ex, TransactionFailedCodes.CREATE_FAILED);
1919                        }
1920                        else
1921                        {
1922                                throw ExceptionBuilder.transactionFailedException("Persistence exception: " + ex, TransactionFailedCodes.UPDATE_FAILED);
1923                        }
1924                }
1925                finally
1926                {
1927                        if (!committed)
1928                        {
1929                                Transaction.rollback();
1930                        }
1931                }
1932                return property;
1933        }
1934 
1935//Getters
1936        /**
1937         *  Get the exchangePrescribedWidth structs for the given exchangeKey/classKey combination.
1938         *
1939         */
1940        public EPWStruct[] getExchangePrescribedWidth(String sessionName, int classKey, org.omg.CORBA.IntHolder seq)
1941                throws SystemException, CommunicationException, DataValidationException, AuthorizationException
1942        {
1943                validateSessionName(sessionName);
1944                validateClassKey(classKey);
1945 
1946                int type = TradingPropertyTypes.EPW_STRUCT;
1947                TradingProperty[] properties;
1948                properties = getTradingPropertyHome().findProperties(sessionName, classKey, type);
1949                if (properties.length == 0 && classKey != ProductClass.DEFAULT_CLASS_KEY)
1950                {
1951                        properties = getTradingPropertyHome().findProperties(sessionName, ProductClass.DEFAULT_CLASS_KEY, type);
1952                }
1953                EPWStruct[] structArray = new EPWStruct[properties.length];
1954                for (int i=0; i < properties.length; i++)
1955                {
1956                        structArray[i] = ((ExchangePrescribedWidth)properties[i]).getEPW();
1957                }
1958                if (properties.length > 0)
1959                {
1960                        seq.value = properties[0].getSequenceId();
1961                }
1962                return structArray;
1963        }

2721        /**

2723         */
2724        public synchronized void setPrescribedWidthRatio (String sessionName, int classKey, double ratio, int seq)
2725                throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, TransactionFailedException
2726        {
2727                boolean committed = false;
2728                Transaction.startTransaction();
2729                try
2730                {
2731                        PrescribedWidthRatio property = (PrescribedWidthRatio)propertyUpdate(sessionName, classKey, TradingPropertyTypes.PRESCRIBED_WIDTH_RATIO, seq);
2732                        property.setRatio(ratio);
2733                        getEventChannelPublisher().acceptPrescribedWidthRatioUpdate(property.getSequenceId(), sessionName, ratio);
2734                        committed = Transaction.commit();
2735                        logPropertyUpdated(property);
2736                }
2737                finally
2738                {
2739                        if (!committed)
2740                        {
2741                                Transaction.rollback();
2742                        }
2743                }
2744        }

2781         *  or else it should be 0 if a new property is expected.
2782         */
2783        public synchronized void setAllocationStrategy(String sessionName, int classKey, AllocationStrategyStruct strategy, int seq)
2784                throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, TransactionFailedException
2785        {

2787            validateSessionName(sessionName);

2793 
2794            if(allStrategies.length == 0)
2795            {
2796                allStrategies = AllocationStrategyHelper.toV2StructSequence(strategy);
2797            }
2798            else
2799            {
2800                allStrategies = AllocationStrategyHelper.consolidateWithDefaultStrategy(allStrategies, strategy);
2801            }
2802 
2803            setAllocationStrategies(sessionName, classKey, allStrategies, seq);
2804        }
2805    /**
2806         *  Set the property's value, either by updating or creating a new property.

2808         *  or else it should be 0 if a new property is expected.

3327         */
3328        public synchronized void setExchangePrescribedWidth(String sessionName, int classKey, EPWStruct[] newEPWs, int seq)
3329                throws SystemException, CommunicationException, DataValidationException, AuthorizationException, TransactionFailedException
3330        {
3331                validateSessionName(sessionName);
3332                validateClassKey(classKey);
3333 
3334                ExchangePrescribedWidthHelper.validateEPW(newEPWs, minSpreadRequired, maxAllowableMaximumBid);
3335 
3336                //  Find current stored values
3337                //
3338                TradingProperty[] properties = getTradingPropertyHome().findProperties(sessionName, classKey, TradingPropertyTypes.EPW_STRUCT);
3339 
3340                // Validate the sequence number:
3341                //
3342                int newSeq = 0;
3343            if (properties.length > 0)
3344            {
3345                newSeq = properties[0].getSequenceId();
3346                Log.information(this,  UPDATE_HEADER + properties[0].getPropertyTypeDescription()
3347                    + ". Existing values: "
3348                    + " sessionName: " + sessionName
3349                    + " classKey: " + classKey
3350                    + " values: " + toStringEPWs(properties));
3351                    }
3352            else
3353            {
3354                Log.information(this,  CREATE_HEADER + "ExchangePrescribedWidth for sessionName: "
3355                    + sessionName
3356                    + " classKey: " + classKey);
3357            }
3358                if (newSeq != seq && newSeq > 0)
3359                {
3360                        throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Expected sequence #" + newSeq + ", got " + seq, DataValidationCodes.INVALID_UPDATE_ATTEMPT);
3361                }
3362                else
3363                {
3364                // If the db is 0 assume that the get returned the default and sequence number should be 0
3365                // or the correct sequence number was passed
3366                // Update list.
3367                //
3368                boolean committed = false;
3369                Transaction.startTransaction();
3370                try
3371                {
3372                       ++newSeq;
3373                        for (int i=0; i < newEPWs.length; i++)
3374                        {
3375                                ExchangePrescribedWidth property;
3376                                if (i < properties.length)
3377                                {
3378                                        property = (ExchangePrescribedWidth)properties[i];
3379                                }
3380                                else // have to create a new one:
3381                                {
3382                                        property = (ExchangePrescribedWidth)getTradingPropertyHome().createProperty(sessionName, TradingPropertyTypes.EPW_STRUCT);
3383                                        property.setClassKey(classKey);
3384                                        property.setSessionName(sessionName);
3385                                }
3386                                property.setEPW(newEPWs[i]);
3387                                property.setSequenceId(newSeq);
3388                        }
3389                        for (int i=newEPWs.length; i < properties.length; i++)
3390                        {
3391                                properties[i].getPersistentProperty().markForDelete();
3392                        }
3393                        getEventChannelPublisher().acceptExchangePrescribedWidthUpdate(newSeq, sessionName, classKey, newEPWs);
3394                        committed = Transaction.commit();
3395                        properties = getTradingPropertyHome().findProperties(sessionName, classKey, TradingPropertyTypes.EPW_STRUCT);
3396                        logPropertyUpdated(toStringEPWs(properties));
3397                }
3398                catch (PersistenceException ex)
3399                {
3400                        throw ExceptionBuilder.transactionFailedException("Failed to set/update EPWStructs: " + ex, TransactionFailedCodes.UPDATE_FAILED);
3401                }
3402                finally
3403                {
3404                        if (!committed)
3405                        {
3406                                Transaction.rollback();
3407                        }
3408                }
3409               }
3410        }
3411

3863    public void setAuctionTimeToLive(String sessionName, int classKey, AuctionRangeStruct[] timeRange, int seq)
3864            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, TransactionFailedException
3865    {
3866        validateSessionName(sessionName);
3867        validateClassKey(classKey);
3868 
3869        TradingProperty[] properties = getTradingPropertyHome().findProperties(sessionName, classKey, TradingPropertyTypes.AUCTION_TIME_TO_LIVE);
3870 
3871        int newSeq = 0;
3872        if (properties.length > 0)
3873        {
3874            newSeq = properties[0].getSequenceId();
3875            Log.information(this,  UPDATE_HEADER + properties[0].getPropertyTypeDescription()
3876                    + ". Existing values: ");
3877            for (int i=0; i<properties.length; i++)
3878            {
3879                logPropertyUpdated(properties[i]);
3880            }
3881        }
3882        else
3883        {
3884            Log.information(this,  CREATE_HEADER + "AuctionTimeToLive for sessionName: "
3885                    + sessionName + " classKey: " + classKey);
3886        }
3887 
3888        if (newSeq != seq && newSeq > 0)
3889        {
3890            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Expected sequence #" + newSeq + ", got " + seq, DataValidationCodes.INVALID_UPDATE_ATTEMPT);
3891        }
3892        else
3893        {
3894            boolean committed = false;
3895            Transaction.startTransaction();
3896            try
3897            {
3898                ++newSeq;
3899                for (int i=0; i<timeRange.length; i++)
3900                {
3901                    if (timeRange[i].lowerLimit < 0 || timeRange[i].upperLimit < 0)
3902                    {
3903                        throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("lowerLimit or upperLimit cannot < 0: lowerLimit: " + timeRange[i].lowerLimit + " upperLimit: " + timeRange[i].upperLimit, DataValidationCodes.INVALID_QUANTITY);
3904                    }
3905                    if (timeRange[i].lowerLimit > timeRange[i].upperLimit)
3906                    {
3907                        throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("lowerLimit cannot > upperLimit: lowerLimit: " + timeRange[i].lowerLimit + " upperLimit: " + timeRange[i].upperLimit, DataValidationCodes.INVALID_QUANTITY);
3908                    }
3909 
3910                    AuctionTimeToLive property;
3911                    if (i<properties.length)
3912                    {
3913                        property = (AuctionTimeToLive)properties[i];
3914                    }
3915                    else
3916                    {
3917                        property = (AuctionTimeToLive)getTradingPropertyHome().createProperty(sessionName, TradingPropertyTypes.AUCTION_TIME_TO_LIVE);
3918                        property.setClassKey(classKey);
3919                        property.setSessionName(sessionName);
3920                    }
3921                    property.setAuctionTimeToLive(timeRange[i]);
3922                    property.setSequenceId(newSeq);
3923                    logPropertyUpdated(property);
3924                }
3925 
3926                for (int i=timeRange.length; i<properties.length; i++)
3927                {
3928                    properties[i].getPersistentProperty().markForDelete();
3929                }
3930                getEventChannelPublisher().acceptAuctionTimeToLiveUpdate(newSeq, sessionName, classKey, timeRange);
3931                committed = Transaction.commit();
3932            }
3933            catch (PersistenceException e)
3934            {
3935                throw ExceptionBuilder.transactionFailedException("Failed to set/update AuctionTimeToLive: " + e, TransactionFailedCodes.UPDATE_FAILED);
3936            }
3937            finally
3938            {
3939                if (!committed)
3940                {

3943            }

4549    private void handleResultString(String result) throws CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, SystemException, DataValidationException, TransactionFailedException, NotFoundException
4550    {
4551        if(!result.equals(""))
4552        {
4553            if(result.indexOf("AuthorizationException") != -1 )
4554            {
4555                throw  ExceptionBuilder.authorizationException(result, 0);
4556            }
4557            else if(result.indexOf("CommunicationException") != -1 )
4558            {
4559                throw  ExceptionBuilder.communicationException(result, 0);
4560            }
4561            else if(result.indexOf("SystemException") != -1 )
4562            {
4563                throw  ExceptionBuilder.systemException(result, 0);
4564            }
4565            else if(result.indexOf("DataValidationException") != -1 )
4566            {
4567                throw  ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException (result, 0);
4568            }
4569            else if(result.indexOf("TransactionFailedException") != -1 )
4570            {
4571                throw  ExceptionBuilder.transactionFailedException(result, 0);
4572            }
4573            else if(result.indexOf("NotFoundException") != -1 )
4574            {
4575                throw  ExceptionBuilder.notFoundException(result, 0);
4576            }
4577        }
4578    }
4579 
4580    /**
4581     *   Removes the property's value from the database and replaces with the default.
4582     *
4583     */
4584 
4585        public synchronized void removeTradingProperty(String sessionName, int classKey,int propertyType)
4586                throws CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, SystemException, DataValidationException, TransactionFailedException, NotFoundException
4587        {
4588                validateSessionName(sessionName);
4589                validateClassKey(classKey);
4590 
4591                try
4592               {
4593 
4594 
4595                    // check if it should use property service, as we always should.  It knows how to do
4596                    // add, update and delete for a given trading property that was used to be maintained
4597                    // by this class.
4598 
4599                    // please note that all trading properties type and names should be defined
4600                    // for PropertyService in TradingPropertyTypeImpl.
4601                    // new trading property should also be added to TradingPropertyFactoryImpl
4602                if ( TradingPropertyFactoryHome.find().getPropertyName( propertyType ).compareTo( TradingPropertyType.PROPERTY_TYPE_NOT_DEFINED ) != 0 )
4603                {
4604                    PropertyServiceHome priopertyServiceHome = getPropertyServiceHome();
4605 
4606                    if( PropertyTradingPropertyServiceHome.class.isInstance( propertyServiceHome ) )
4607                    {
4608                        PropertyTradingPropertyServiceHome propertyTradingPriopertyServiceHome = (PropertyTradingPropertyServiceHome)propertyServiceHome;
4609                        String result = propertyTradingPriopertyServiceHome.adminRemoveTradingProperty( sessionName, ""+classKey, propertyType );
4610                        handleResultString(result);
4611                    }
4612                    else
4613                    {
4614                        throw ExceptionBuilder.systemException( "PropertyServiceHome NOT instance of PropertyTradingPropertySerivceHome ==>> Unsupported property type: " + propertyType, 0 );
4615                    }
4616                }
4617                else
4618                {
4619                    Log.alarm(this, "Calling remove trading property."
4620                            + " This should have been using PropertyTradingPropertyService."
4621                            + " Unless it is not configured. Performing removal anyway for "
4622                            + " sessionName:classKey:propertyType "
4623                            + sessionName + ":" + classKey + ":" + propertyType);
4624 
4625                TradingProperty[] property = getTradingPropertyHome().findProperties(sessionName, classKey, propertyType);
4626 
4627                  if (property[0] != null)
4628                  {
4629                    if (property[0].getClassKey() != ProductClass.DEFAULT_CLASS_KEY)
4630                      {
4631                        for (int i=0;i < property.length; i++)
4632                        {
4633                          logPropertyRemoved(property[i]);
4634                          getTradingPropertyHome().remove(property[i]);
4635                          publishRemoveTradingPropertyEvent(sessionName, classKey, propertyType);
4636                        }
4637                      }
4638                    else
4639                    {
4640                    throw ExceptionBuilder.transactionFailedException("Cannot remove DEFAULT CLASS property: ", 0);
4641                     }
4642                    }
4643                  }
4644               }
4645                  catch (SystemException ex)
4646                  {
4647                    throw ExceptionBuilder.transactionFailedException("Delete exception: " + ex, TransactionFailedCodes.UPDATE_FAILED);
4648                  }
4649                 finally
4650                  {
4651                    }
4652        }
4653/* All Classes */
4654/**
4655 *   Get all exchangePrescribedWidth structs for all classes in the system.
4656 *   Does not return EPW structs for the default class key.
4657 *
4658 *   <p><b>Note: </b> this method is a little expensive: hopefully it will not be called very often.
4659 *   <p><b>Note: </b> careful with the sequence numbers!
4660 */
4661        public SpreadClassStruct[] getExchangePrescribedWidthForAllClasses(String sessionName)
4662                throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException,DataValidationException
4663        {
4664                // Find all EPWStructs, organize them by class.
4665                //
4666                validateSessionName(sessionName);
4667                TradingProperty[] properties = getTradingPropertyHome().findPropertiesForAllClasses(sessionName, TradingPropertyTypes.EPW_STRUCT);
4668                IntHashMap classMap = new IntHashMap();
4669                for (int i=0; i < properties.length; i++)
4670                {
4671                    ExchangePrescribedWidth property = (ExchangePrescribedWidth)properties[i];
4672                    EpwSequenceWrapper wrapper = (EpwSequenceWrapper)classMap.get(property.getClassKey());
4673                    if(wrapper == null){
4674                        wrapper = new EpwSequenceWrapper(property.getSequenceId());
4675                       classMap.put(property.getClassKey(),wrapper);
4676                    }
4677                    wrapper.addEpwStruct(property.getEPW());
4678                  }
4679 
4680                // Fill in the result struct.
4681                //
4682            SpreadClassStruct[] epwClassStructs = new SpreadClassStruct[classMap.size()];
4683                Set keySet = classMap.keySet();
4684                Iterator keyIter = keySet.iterator();
4685                for (int i=0; i < epwClassStructs.length; i++)
4686                {
4687                        epwClassStructs[i] = new SpreadClassStruct();
4688                        Integer intObj = (Integer)keyIter.next();
4689                        EpwSequenceWrapper epwSeq =(EpwSequenceWrapper)classMap.get(intObj.intValue());
4690                        epwClassStructs[i] = new SpreadClassStruct();
4691                        epwClassStructs[i].classKey = intObj.intValue();
4692                        epwClassStructs[i].seqNum = epwSeq.getSequenceId();
4693                        Vector widths = epwSeq.getWidths();
4694                        epwClassStructs[i].spreads = new EPWStruct[widths.size()];
4695                        widths.copyInto(epwClassStructs[i].spreads);
4696                }
4697                return epwClassStructs;
4698 
4699        }
4700    class EpwSequenceWrapper {
4701        int sequenceId;
4702        Vector list;
4703 
4704        public EpwSequenceWrapper(int s){
4705            sequenceId = s;
4706            list = new Vector();
4707        }
4708        public synchronized void addEpwStruct(EPWStruct e){
4709            list.addElement(e);
4710        }
4711        public Vector getWidths(){
4712            return list;
4713        }
4714        public int getSequenceId(){
4715            return sequenceId;
4716        }
4717    }
4718    /** DEPRECATED: use getAllocationStrategiesForAllClasses instead*/
4719      public AllocationStrategyClassStruct[] getAllocationStrategyForAllClasses(java.lang.String sessionName)
4720        throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotFoundException
4721      {
4722         validateSessionName(sessionName);
4723         TradingProperty[] properties = getTradingPropertyHome().findPropertiesForAllClasses(sessionName,TradingPropertyTypes.ALLOCATION_STRATEGY);
4724         IntHashMap allocPropMap = new IntHashMap();
4725         // Walk through results of get all and build hashmap with key of class
4726         for (int i = 0; i < properties.length; i++)
4727         {
4728            AllocationStrategy property = (AllocationStrategy)properties[i];
4729            
4730            Vector allocProps = (Vector)allocPropMap.get(property.getClassKey());
4731            // When the list of properties has ended for the class add to map
4732              if (allocProps == null)
4733               {
4734                  allocProps = new Vector();
4735                  allocPropMap.put(property.getClassKey(), allocProps);
4736               }
4737            // Add to the vector per class
4738              allocProps.addElement(property);
4739         }
4740        //
4741        AllocationStrategyClassStruct[] allocClassStructs = new AllocationStrategyClassStruct[allocPropMap.size()];
4742        Set keySet = allocPropMap.keySet();
4743        Iterator keyIter = keySet.iterator();
4744         if (allocClassStructs.length > 0)
4745             {
4746              for (int j = 0; j < allocClassStructs.length; j++)
4747              {
4748                 Integer intObj = (Integer) keyIter.next();
4749                 Vector allocations = (Vector) allocPropMap.get(intObj.intValue());
4750                 allocClassStructs[j] = new AllocationStrategyClassStruct();
4751                 allocClassStructs[j].classKey = intObj.intValue();
4752                 //first element of this vector is the  sequence number
4753                 allocClassStructs[j].seqNum = ((AllocationStrategy)allocations.firstElement()).getSequenceId();
4754 
4755                 TradingProperty[] allocProperties = (TradingProperty[])allocations.toArray(new TradingProperty[allocations.size()]);
4756                 allocClassStructs[j].allocationStrategy = getAllocationStrategyCodes(allocProperties);
4757                }
4758              }
4759              else
4760              {
4761                 throw ExceptionBuilder.notFoundException("Allocation strategy not found", 0);
4762              }
4763         return allocClassStructs;
4764      }

5182    public DpmRightsScaleClassStruct[] getDpmRightsScaleForAllClasses(String sessionName)
5183        throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException
5184    {
5185        validateSessionName(sessionName);
5186        TradingProperty[] properties = getTradingPropertyHome().findPropertiesForAllClasses(sessionName,TradingPropertyTypes.DPM_RIGHTS_SCALES);
5187        IntHashMap allocPropMap = new IntHashMap();
5188        // Walk through results of get all and build hashmap with key of class
5189        for (int i = 0; i < properties.length; i++)
5190        {
5191           DPMRightsScale property = (DPMRightsScale)properties[i];
5192           int classKey = property.getClassKey();
5193 
5194           Vector allocProps = (Vector)allocPropMap.get(classKey);
5195           // When the list of properties has ended for the class add to map
5196             if (allocProps == null)
5197              {
5198                 allocProps = new Vector();
5199                 allocPropMap.put(classKey, allocProps);
5200              }
5201           // Add to the vector per class
5202             allocProps.addElement(property);
5203        }
5204        // get trading allocation strategies for each class
5205        DpmRightsScaleClassStruct[] scaleStructs = new DpmRightsScaleClassStruct[allocPropMap.size()];
5206        Set keySet = allocPropMap.keySet();
5207        Iterator keyIter = keySet.iterator();
5208        Integer intObj = null;
5209        IntHolder seq = null;
5210        if (scaleStructs.length > 0)
5211        {
5212             for (int j = 0; j < scaleStructs.length; j++)
5213             {
5214                intObj = (Integer) keyIter.next();
5215                seq = new IntHolder();
5216                scaleStructs[j] = new DpmRightsScaleClassStruct();
5217                scaleStructs[j].classKey = intObj.intValue();
5218                scaleStructs[j].scales = this.getDpmRightsScales(sessionName, intObj.intValue(), seq);
5219                scaleStructs[j].seqNum = seq.value;
5220              }
5221         }
5222        return scaleStructs;
5223    }
5224

5456                        getEventChannelPublisher().acceptAutoExEligibleStrategyTypesUpdate(intHolder.value, sessionName, classKey, eligibleTypes);
5457                        break;
5458                    case TradingPropertyTypes.AUCTION_ENABLED:
5459                        AuctionBooleanStruct[] enabled = this.getAuctionEnabled(sessionName, defaultClassKey, intHolder);
5460                        getEventChannelPublisher().acceptAuctionEnabledUpdate(intHolder.value, sessionName, classKey, enabled);
5461                        break;
5462                    case TradingPropertyTypes.AUCTION_MIN_ORDER_SIZE_FOR_TICKS_ABOVE_NBBO:
5463                        AuctionOrderSizeTicksStruct[] sizeTicks = this.getAuctionMinOrderSizeForTicksAboveNBBO(sessionName, defaultClassKey, intHolder);
5464                        getEventChannelPublisher().acceptAuctionMinOrderSizeForTicksAboveNBBOUpdate(intHolder.value, sessionName, classKey, sizeTicks);
5465                        break;
5466                    default:
5467                        Log.information("Cannot remove property: Invalid tradingPropertyType=" + tradingPropertyType);
5468                }
5469            }
5470            catch (Exception e)
5471            {
5472                Log.exception(e);
5473            }
5474     }

5476     public void setAllocationStrategies(String sessionName, int classKey, AllocationStrategyStructV2[] allocationStrategyStructV2s, int seq)
5477                 throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, TransactionFailedException, DataValidationException
5478         {
5479             validateSessionName(sessionName);
5480             validateClassKey(classKey);
5481 
5482             validateAllocationStrategies(allocationStrategyStructV2s);
5483             AllocationValidationStrategy allocationValidationStrategy = getAllocationValidationStrategy(sessionName);
5484             allocationValidationStrategy.validateAllocationStrategies(allocationStrategyStructV2s);
5485             //  Find current stored values
5486             //
5487             TradingProperty[] properties = getTradingPropertyHome().findProperties(sessionName, classKey, TradingPropertyTypes.ALLOCATION_STRATEGY);
5488 
5489             // Validate the sequence number:
5490                     //
5491             int newSeq = 0;
5492             if (properties.length > 0)
5493             {
5494                 newSeq = properties[0].getSequenceId();
5495                 Log.information(this, UPDATE_HEADER + properties[0].getPropertyTypeDescription()
5496                         + ". Existing values: "
5497                         + " sessionName: " + sessionName
5498                         + " classKey: " + classKey
5499                         + " values: " + toStringAllocationStrategies(sessionName, classKey));
5500             }
5501             else
5502             {
5503                 Log.information(this,  CREATE_HEADER + "AllocationStrategy for sessionName: "
5504                         + sessionName
5505                         + " classKey: " + classKey);
5506             }
5507             if (newSeq != seq && newSeq > 0)
5508             {
5509                     throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Expected sequence #" + newSeq + ", got " + seq, DataValidationCodes.INVALID_UPDATE_ATTEMPT);
5510             }
5511 
5512             // Update list.
5513             //
5514             boolean committed = false;
5515             Transaction.startTransaction();
5516             try
5517             {
5518                 int totalLength = getTotalEntryLength(allocationStrategyStructV2s);
5519                 int previousSectionLength = 0;
5520                 int singleLength = 0;
5521                 ++newSeq;
5522                 for(int n = 0; n < allocationStrategyStructV2s.length; n++)
5523                 {
5524                     singleLength = singleLength + allocationStrategyStructV2s[n].prioritizedStrategyCodes.length + 1;
5525 
5526                     int currentPrioritiyIndex = 0;
5527                     for (int i = previousSectionLength; i < singleLength  ; i++)
5528                     {
5529                         AllocationStrategy property;
5530                         if (i < properties.length)
5531                         {
5532                             property = (AllocationStrategy) properties[i];
5533                         }
5534                         else // have to create a new one:
5535                         {
5536                             property = (AllocationStrategy) getTradingPropertyHome().createProperty(sessionName, TradingPropertyTypes.ALLOCATION_STRATEGY);
5537                             property.setClassKey(classKey);
5538                             property.setSessionName(sessionName);
5539                         }
5540                         if (i == previousSectionLength)
5541                         {
5542                             property.setIndex(-1);
5543                             property.setCode(allocationStrategyStructV2s[n].defaultStrategyCode);
5544                             property.setType(allocationStrategyStructV2s[n].allocationTradeType);
5545                         }
5546                         else
5547                         {
5548                             property.setIndex(currentPrioritiyIndex - 1 );
5549                             property.setCode(allocationStrategyStructV2s[n].prioritizedStrategyCodes[currentPrioritiyIndex - 1]);
5550                             property.setType(allocationStrategyStructV2s[n].allocationTradeType);
5551                         }
5552                         currentPrioritiyIndex++;
5553                         property.setSequenceId(newSeq);
5554                     }
5555                     previousSectionLength = singleLength;
5556                 }
5557 
5558 
5559                 for (int i= totalLength; i < properties.length; i++)
5560                 {
5561                     properties[i].getPersistentProperty().markForDelete();
5562                 }
5563 
5564                 getEventChannelPublisher().acceptAllocationStrategiesUpdate(newSeq, sessionName, classKey, allocationStrategyStructV2s);
5565                 committed = Transaction.commit();
5566                 logPropertyUpdated(toStringAllocationStrategies(sessionName, classKey));
5567             }
5568             catch (PersistenceException ex)
5569             {
5570                     throw ExceptionBuilder.transactionFailedException("Failed to set/update allocation strategies " + ex, TransactionFailedCodes.UPDATE_FAILED);
5571             }
5572             finally
5573             {
5574                     if (!committed)
5575                     {
5576                             Transaction.rollback();
5577                     }
5578             }
5579         }

5581         public AllocationStrategyStructV2[] getAllocationStrategies(String sessionName, int classKey, IntHolder seq)
5582                     throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException
5583             {
5584                 validateSessionName(sessionName);
5585                 validateClassKey(classKey);
5586                 int type = TradingPropertyTypes.ALLOCATION_STRATEGY;
5587                 TradingProperty[] properties;
5588                 properties = getTradingPropertyHome().findProperties(sessionName, classKey, type);
5589                 if (properties.length == 0 && classKey != ProductClass.DEFAULT_CLASS_KEY)
5590                 {
5591                     properties = getTradingPropertyHome().findProperties(sessionName, ProductClass.DEFAULT_CLASS_KEY, type);
5592                 }
5593                 if (properties.length > 0)
5594                 {
5595                     seq.value = properties[0].getSequenceId();
5596                     AllocationStrategyStructV2 resultElement = null;
5597                     Collection sortedByTypeProperties = groupAllocationPropertiesByType(properties);
5598 
5599                     AllocationStrategyStructV2[] result = new AllocationStrategyStructV2[sortedByTypeProperties.size()];
5600                     ArrayList listForType = null;
5601                     AllocationStrategy strategyProperty = null;
5602                     Iterator groupedProperties = sortedByTypeProperties.iterator();
5603                     int i = 0;
5604                     while(groupedProperties.hasNext())
5605                     {
5606                         listForType = (ArrayList)groupedProperties.next();
5607                         resultElement = new AllocationStrategyStructV2();
5608                         resultElement.prioritizedStrategyCodes = new short[listForType.size() - 1]; // remove one for default code
5609 
5610                         for (int j = 0; j < listForType.size(); j++)
5611                         {
5612                             strategyProperty = (AllocationStrategy) listForType.get(j);
5613                             if (strategyProperty.getIndex() == -1)
5614                             {
5615                                 resultElement.defaultStrategyCode = strategyProperty.getCode();
5616                                 resultElement.allocationTradeType = strategyProperty.getType();
5617                             }
5618                             else
5619                             {
5620                                 resultElement.prioritizedStrategyCodes[strategyProperty.getIndex()] = strategyProperty.getCode();
5621                                 resultElement.allocationTradeType = strategyProperty.getType();
5622                             }
5623                         }
5624                         result[i++] = resultElement;
5625                     }
5626                     return result;
5627                 }
5628                 else
5629                 {
5630                     return new AllocationStrategyStructV2[0];
5631                 }
5632             }
5633 
5634             private int getTotalEntryLength(AllocationStrategyStructV2[] allocationStrategyStructV2s)
5635             {
5636                 int newLength = 0;
5637                 for(int i = 0; i <allocationStrategyStructV2s.length; i++ )
5638                 {
5639                     newLength = newLength + (allocationStrategyStructV2s[i].prioritizedStrategyCodes.length) + 1; // +1 is for default code
5640                 }
5641 
5642                 return newLength;
5643             }
5644 
5645            /** this is coded for AllocationStrategy only grouped by type
5646             * */
5647             private Collection groupAllocationPropertiesByType(TradingProperty[] properties)
5648             {
5649                    IntHashMap groupedList = new IntHashMap();
5650 
5651                    ArrayList listOfSameType = null;
5652 
5653                    for(int i = 0; i < properties.length; i++ )
5654                    {
5655                        int currentType = ((AllocationStrategy) properties[i]).getType();
5656                        listOfSameType = (ArrayList)groupedList.get(currentType);
5657                        if(listOfSameType == null)
5658                        {
5659                            listOfSameType = new ArrayList();
5660                            groupedList.put(currentType, listOfSameType);
5661                        }
5662 
5663                        listOfSameType.add(properties[i]);
5664                     }
5665 
5666 
5667                    return groupedList.values();
5668              }
5669

5671    /**
5672     * 
5673     * Get the validation strategy for validating the allocation strategy trading property.
5674     * @param sessionName
5675     * @return
5676     */
5677    protected AllocationValidationStrategy getAllocationValidationStrategy(String sessionName)
5678    {
5679            AllocationValidationStrategy allocationValidationStrategy = allocationValidationStrategies.get(sessionName);
5680            if(allocationValidationStrategy == null)
5681            {
5682                    try {
5683                                    String className = "com.cboe.internalBusinessServices.tradingPropertyService.AllocationValidation"+sessionName+"Strategy";
5684                                        allocationValidationStrategy = (AllocationValidationStrategy)(Class.forName(className)).newInstance();
5685                                        allocationValidationStrategies.put(sessionName, allocationValidationStrategy);
5686                                } catch (Exception e) {
5687                                Log.information("TradingPropertyServiceLocalImpl >> No Strategy Defined for validating the AllocationStrategy trading Property for "
5688                                                                + sessionName+ " session. Using the default strategy :AllocationValidationDefaultStrategy");
5689                                allocationValidationStrategy = defaultAllocationValidationStrategy;
5690                                allocationValidationStrategies.put(sessionName,defaultAllocationValidationStrategy);
5691                        }
5692            }
5693                return allocationValidationStrategy;
5694    }

7154    protected String toStringAllocationType(short tradeType)
7155    {
7156       String type = "Unknown";
7157       switch (tradeType)
7158       {
7159            case AllocationTradeTypes.REGULAR:
7160               type = "Regular Trade";
7161               break;
7162            case AllocationTradeTypes.QUOTE_TRIGGER:
7163               type = "Quote Trigger Trade";
7164               break;
7165            case AllocationTradeTypes.OPENING:
7166               type = "Opening Trade";
7167               break;
7168            default:
7169               type = "Unknown";
7170       }
7171       return type;
7172    }

7174    protected String toStringAllocationStrategies( String session, int classKey)
7175    {
7176        StringBuffer codes = new StringBuffer();
7177        try
7178        {
7179            AllocationStrategyStructV2[] strategies = getAllocationStrategies(session, classKey, new IntHolder());
7180            for(int i = 0; i < strategies.length; i++)
7181            {
7182                if(i != 0)
7183                {
7184                    codes.append(", ");
7185                }
7186                codes.append("" + strategies[i].allocationTradeType);
7187                codes.append("(" + toStringAllocationType(strategies[i].allocationTradeType) + ")");
7188                codes.append(" is " + strategies[i].defaultStrategyCode);
7189                for (int j = 0; j < strategies[i].prioritizedStrategyCodes.length; j++) {
7190                    codes.append(";" + strategies[i].prioritizedStrategyCodes[j]);
7191                }
7192            }
7193        }
7194        catch(Exception e)
7195        {
7196            Log.exception(this, e);
7197            codes = new StringBuffer("Error getting AllocationStrategies");
7198        }
7199        return codes.toString();
7200    }
7201    protected String toStringEPWs(TradingProperty[] newEPWs)
7202    {
7203        String str = "UNKNOWN";
7204        ExchangePrescribedWidth property;
7205        EPWStruct epwStruct;
7206        if(newEPWs ==null || newEPWs.length == 0)
7207        {
7208            return str;
7209        }
7210        try
7211        {
7212            StringBuffer buf = new StringBuffer();
7213                        for (int i=0; i < newEPWs.length; i++)
7214                        {
7215                property = (ExchangePrescribedWidth)newEPWs[i];
7216                epwStruct = property.getEPW();
7217                if(i !=0)
7218                {
7219                    buf.append("; ");
7220                }
7221                buf.append(epwStruct.minimumBidRange);
7222                buf.append(" - ");
7223                buf.append(epwStruct.maximumBidRange);
7224                buf.append(" spread: ");
7225                buf.append(epwStruct.maximumAllowableSpread);
7226                        }
7227            str = buf.toString();
7228        }
7229        catch(Exception e)
7230        {
7231            Log.exception(this, e);
7232        }
7233        return str;
7234    }

7245        try
7246        {
7247            StringBuffer buf = new StringBuffer();
7248                        for (int i=0; i < newScales.length; i++)
7249                        {
7250                property = (DPMRightsScale)newScales[i];
7251                struct = property.getDpmRightsScale();
7252                if(i !=0)
7253                {
7254                    buf.append("; ");
7255                }
7256                buf.append(" if >= ");
7257                buf.append(struct.lowNbrParticipants);
7258                buf.append(" < ");
7259                buf.append(struct.highNbrParticipants);
7260                buf.append(" scale: ");
7261                buf.append(struct.scalePercentage);
7262                        }
7263            str = buf.toString();
7264        }
7265        catch(Exception e)
7266        {
7267            Log.exception(this, e);
7268        }
7269        return str;
7270    }

7298    public synchronized void setQuoteLockMinimumTradeQuantity(java.lang.String sessionName, int classKey, int size, int seq)
7299            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, TransactionFailedException, DataValidationException
7300    {
7301        boolean committed = false;
7302        Transaction.startTransaction();
7303        try
7304        {
7305                QuoteLockMinimumTradeQuantity property = (QuoteLockMinimumTradeQuantity)propertyUpdate(sessionName, classKey, TradingPropertyTypes.QUOTE_LOCK_MIN_TRADE_QTY, seq);
7306                property.setQuoteLockMinimumTradeQuantity(size);
7307                getEventChannelPublisher().acceptQuoteLockMinimumTradeQuantityUpdate(property.getSequenceId(), sessionName, classKey, size);
7308                committed = Transaction.commit();
7309                logPropertyUpdated(property);
7310        }
7311        finally
7312        {
7313                if (!committed)
7314                {
7315                        Transaction.rollback();
7316                }
7317        }
7318    }

7383    private void adminPublishIPPToleranceAmount(String sessionName, int msgPerSecond){
7384        Log.information("TradingPropertyServiceLocalImpl >> starting publishing IPPToleranceAmount for session: " + sessionName);
7385        int msgPublished = 0;
7386        int total = 0;
7387        try {
7388            DoubleStruct[] properties = getIPPToleranceAmountForAllClasses(sessionName);
7389            total = properties.length;
7390            long startTime = System.currentTimeMillis();
7391            int defaultClassIndex = -1;
7392            for (int i = 0; i < properties.length; i++) {
7393                if (properties[i].classKey == ProductClass.DEFAULT_CLASS_KEY) {
7394                    defaultClassIndex = i;
7395                    break;
7396                }
7397            }
7398            DoubleStruct property;
7399            if ( defaultClassIndex != -1) {
7400                property = properties[defaultClassIndex];
7401                getEventChannelPublisher().acceptIPPToleranceAmountUpdate((property.seqNum), sessionName, property.classKey, property.doubleValue );
7402                msgPublished++;
7403            }
7404            for (int i = 0; i < properties.length; i++){
7405                if (i != defaultClassIndex) {

7408                    msgPublished++;

7410                        startTime = System.currentTimeMillis();
7411                    }

7413            }
7414        }

7497    private boolean adminControlMsgRate(int msgPerSecond, int msgPublished, long startTime) {
7498        boolean waited = false;
7499        try {
7500            if (msgPublished % msgPerSecond == 0) {
7501                long millsLeft = 1000 - (System.currentTimeMillis() - startTime);
7502                if (millsLeft > 0 ) {
7503                    wait(millsLeft);
7504                    waited = true;
7505                }
7506            }
7507        }
7508        catch (Exception e) {
7509            Log.exception("TradingPropertyServiceLocalImpl >> adminControlMsgRate", e);
7510        }
7511        return waited;
7512    }
